<div id="review_146697590" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/146697590" />
    <a title="Nairabell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1954980-nairabell"><img alt="Nairabell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1356530495p2/1954980.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/146697590?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nairabell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nairabell" href="/user/show/1954980-nairabell">Nairabell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781847384997" href="/book/show/7936576-the-haunted">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1954980-nairabell?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1954980-nairabell?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1954980-nairabell?shelf=teen-ya-paranormal">teen-ya-paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer146697590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4820217697918849819">Abbey has been desperately trying to forget Caspian, the boy she fell in love with only to discover he was already dead. Traumatised by the discovery and doubting her sanity Abbey left Sleepy Hollow for the summer, but now the summer is over and it is time for Abbey to return. At first she throws herself into her schoolwork and concentrates on her friendship with the definitely alive Ben. Then Caspian reappears in her life, and Abbey realises you can't outrun your destiny. <br/><br/>This is the second par</span>
  <span id="freeText4820217697918849819" style="display:none">Abbey has been desperately trying to forget Caspian, the boy she fell in love with only to discover he was already dead. Traumatised by the discovery and doubting her sanity Abbey left Sleepy Hollow for the summer, but now the summer is over and it is time for Abbey to return. At first she throws herself into her schoolwork and concentrates on her friendship with the definitely alive Ben. Then Caspian reappears in her life, and Abbey realises you can't outrun your destiny. <br /><br />This is the second part of a trilogy that started with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6744417.The_Hollow__The_Hollow___1_" title="The Hollow (The Hollow, #1) by Jessica Verday" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hollow</a>. I loved the first book and was blown away by this one. The plot is deeper, with a focus on whether Caspian is real or if Abbey is losing her mind because of the stress of her best friend's death. I've never seen a paranormal book focus on the sanity of the lead character like this before, and it even makes the reader begin to doubt if Caspian is real. <br /><br />All my favourite characters from the first book have returned, along with a selection of new characters. Many of the questions raised in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6744417.The_Hollow__The_Hollow___1_" title="The Hollow (The Hollow, #1) by Jessica Verday" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hollow</a> but not answered are answered here, although more questions are raised and left open. Kristen's secret boyfriend is revealed, Katy and Nicholas reveal how they came to be together and the choices they had to make and a whole new dimension is added with the idea of Revenants. <br /><br />Again, there are twists scattered throughout the story that I didn't see coming and I loved how Abbey and Caspian's relationship developed. The book does have a shocking cliffhanger ending that made me really anxious to get hold of the last part of their story. Without spoilers, it's an incredible ending and I can't wait to see what happens next. <br /><br />All in all this was an amazing read and I'm really looking forward to the final part of the trilogy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10322714.The_Hidden__The_Hollow___3_" title="The Hidden (The Hollow, #3) by Jessica Verday" rel="nofollow noopener">The Hidden</a>) out in September. <br /><br />Plot: 10/10 <br />Characters: 10/10 <br />Ending: 10/10 <br />Enjoyment: 10/10 <br />Cover: 9/10 <br /><br />Overall: 49/50</span>
  <a data-text-id="4820217697918849819" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/434887405?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caidyn (he/him/his)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caidyn (he/him/his)" href="/user/show/13614926-caidyn-he-him-his">Caidyn (he/him/his)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13614926-caidyn-he-him-his?shelf=young-adult-fiction">young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13614926-caidyn-he-him-his?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer434887405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14717087627775588202">Basic summary is that she falls in love with a dead guy and makes friends with people who are really dead and who were in the Sleepy Hollow legend. I liked the idea of being able to talk to the dead as well as sleepy hollow, which is a famous American tale. But, honestly, it turned into a Twilight like tale. When Abbey, the heroine, was around Caspian, or even Ben, it turned cliched and she lost her usual sarcastic spunk that I grew to love in the first book. If you haven’t read the first book, </span>
  <span id="freeText14717087627775588202" style="display:none">Basic summary is that she falls in love with a dead guy and makes friends with people who are really dead and who were in the Sleepy Hollow legend. I liked the idea of being able to talk to the dead as well as sleepy hollow, which is a famous American tale. But, honestly, it turned into a Twilight like tale. When Abbey, the heroine, was around Caspian, or even Ben, it turned cliched and she lost her usual sarcastic spunk that I grew to love in the first book. If you haven’t read the first book, The Hollow, it really goes like this: Her best friend, Kristen, goes missing and is later told to be dead. Abbey makes those friends with Nikolas, Katy, and, her lover, Caspian. At the end it is told that they are all dead and she, basically, loses her grip on sanity. As soon as I read the words about Caspian sneaking into her bedroom when she was gone I couldn’t read anymore of this. I will only recommend it to Twilight-lovers and people who are interested in Sleepy Hollow/the undead and being able to see them. This sequel disappointed me and I won’t be reading the third, The Hidden.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14717087627775588202" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8280630312823340162" style="display:none">Jessica has did it again. The Haunted is an amazing second installment of The Hollow Trilogy. The story of this novel has alot more depth to then The Hollow. Alot of the questions that are left unanswers in The Hollow are answered in The Haunted as well as a few more questions that leave you begging for more.<br /><br />All the main characters that we grew to love in The Hollow are back and there are a few new ones thrown into the mix. Abbey has matured alot and her kind and down to earth nature as easy to connect with. We also get to learn more about Caspian and his story. And it was so easy to see how much he loves Abbey.<br /><br />There is also a few really funny moments as well I was in knots with laughter. Also, a couple of sad moments that brought the tears to my eyes.<br /><br />I recommend this to those to like to read stories that is emotional and gripping.<br /><br />Can't wait for Forever!!!!! It is hard to put myself in her place, because I have no idea how I would react. <br/> Caspian is even more vulnerable and awesome in this one.   <span id="freeText6495849618712294555" style="display:none"> I enjoyed The Hollow even more than the first one! Abbey came even more alive, and I discovered so much more about her. She faces so many decisions, difficulties and trials, I ache for her. It is hard to put myself in her place, because I have no idea how I would react. <br /> Caspian is even more vulnerable and awesome in this one. We find out more about him and it only makes him even more desirable to me. Even though the mystery element is still there, some of my questions are answered and that doesn't detract. <br /> There is lots of conflict in this one and more of the bad guys are emerging. I still have lots of questions, and I am aching for the next books. We still have the character driven literaryness, but there is so much going on. The subplots are woven in really well. <br /> I've enjoyed this series, and recommend it. <br /><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText12922926109564098766" style="display:none">Abbey comes back to Sleepy Hollow, she wants to leave everything behind, but she can't. She throws herself into making her perfumes and has Ben tutor her to try and pass chemistry. She even thinks he may be her answer to get over Caspian. But She can't forget Caspian she thinks of him everywhere she looks and thinks she sees him at every turn she makes. She eventually sees Caspian and realizes she doesn't want to be without him. She works with Ben 2 days a week on chemistry and starts work at her uncles ice cream shop. The rest of the time she spends with Caspian or working on her perfumes and business plan.<br /><br />Strange people have been coming around and when Abbey meets them she gets a strange vibe from them and doesn't understand what they want. They went to Nikolas and Katy for anwers. She ask them what a revenant was, that Vincent said he was one. The told her they are sent to help the half cross over to the Shade half. A shadaw caught between two worlds. They told her she was Caspian's other half, his living half. his partner and companion. "A soul mate." Its called a coupling and we can't say what happens when you and Caspian are completed. Then Katy drops the bomb and tells Abbey that this means she's going to die soon. <br /><br />She realizes how much she loves him but how she isn't ready to die. Caspian reminds her that he is dead and how much better she would be without him and that if they weren't together this wouldn't be happenting. But she tells him he isn't going to do this to her again that he broke her once with the "I only want to be your friend crap" and he wasn't doing that again. She told him before I knew you were dead and after I chose you and I love you. But she decides she needs to see where he is buried and so they take a trip to West Virginia. They only way she can think to make her parents let her go she tells them she is going to see a college there and she wants to go alone, but they want her to go with a friend. It comes out as a joke that Ben can go with her but then the actually agree to it. Caspian tells her she isn't going with out him. Caspian is jealous of Ben and has a hard time in the car. But once at the hotel he and Abbey have the room to themselves. Things get intimate and she realizes why she is so in love with him and he watches over her while she sleeps. That morning she takes a shower and she comes out in a towel and he almost loses control but she says he's not playing fair because he has on clothes. He immediately takes off is shirt and she tells him to wait and runs to the bathroom to get her lotion. When she comes out she takes the towel off her head and shakes out her hair, and the rubs one leg with lotion and Caspain is licking his lips and can barely speak. He tells her she has another leg and she laughs. Then the Ben knocks to ask if she's ready to leave. Caspian tells her it isn't over yet and she tells him promises promises. The next day the take a cab to his home town and he shows her where he grew up. His childhood home, where he played on the railroad tracks, the elementary school he went to, and them of course the cemetery. She thought it would upset her more to see his gravesite, but his was the oppisite. The trip was good for her and they head back home after she leaves some flowers for him. <br /><br />When she gets dropped off by Ben she goes in and finds her parents aren't home waiting for her. But Vincent is in her room and scares her. He is sitting on her bed in the middle of funeral sprays in a black suit with is hair dyed like Caspians. The grabs her and tries to kiss her. She tries to get away and can't. The starts breaking her perfume bottles and then breaks the entire cabinet her parents fixed for the perfumes and she is screaming at him. Caspian comes in and attacks Caspian and they fight. Vincent leaves as the other Revenants come..... They say they are here for me to take me and I know I will be able to be with Caspian, but all I could say to them was "I'm not ready." </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pbsvZlT71p6SGIn5P/cjJG6kBlQ74j+u22Btlvnj5MKlSRFFHgcvlFB8TU7/1rYD+ou79dpZh5bretpvpXePkw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bzpui/gHAgjYht9dNeyq5jyRRaeanOar4kseFWtlqnhvyFCosvv7AhriG+r1zT/BqL74BnsnXpPSUansN/HBKQ==')})
  }
//]]>

She wrote the first draft of THE HOLLOW by hand, using thirteen spiral-bound notebooks and fifteen black pens.
